  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_f869072f-0a4f-4e33-8ae4-4e9f7a13cbf6'
      });

<span id="freeTextContainer4289342414327174128">The race to the Still Blue has reached a stalemate. <i>Aria and Perry are determined to find this last safe haven from the Aether storms before Sable and Hess do—</i>and they are just as determined to stay together.<br/><br/>Within the confines of a cave they're using as a makeshift refuge, they struggle to reconcile their people, Dwellers and Outsiders, who are united only in their hatred</span>
  <span id="freeText4289342414327174128" style="display:none">The race to the Still Blue has reached a stalemate. <i>Aria and Perry are determined to find this last safe haven from the Aether storms before Sable and Hess do—</i>and they are just as determined to stay together.<br /><br />Within the confines of a cave they're using as a makeshift refuge, they struggle to reconcile their people, Dwellers and Outsiders, who are united only in their hatred of their desperate situation. Meanwhile, time is running out to rescue Cinder, who was abducted by Hess and Sable for his unique abilities. Then Roar arrives in a grief-stricken fury, endangering all with his need for revenge.<br /><br />Out of options, Perry and Aria assemble an unlikely team for an impossible rescue mission. Cinder isn't just the key to unlocking the Still Blue and their only hope for survival—he's also their friend. And in a dying world, the bonds between people are what matter most.<br /><br />In this final book in her earth-shattering Under the Never Sky trilogy, Veronica Rossi raises the stakes to their absolute limit and brings her epic love story to an unforgettable close.</span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=i-really-want-to-kiss-the-hero">i-really-want-to-kiss-the-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=slow-burn-romance">slow-burn-romance</a>,

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1304413208" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5937960791308593468">I am currently rereading it for the fifth times! And I’m so torn at the moment. I want to finish reading it and start reading another book in my TBR pile but I also don’t want to finish reading it at the same time because I love it too much! 😫<br/><br/>•••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••<br/><br/><b>
  <u>Fourth Time Read Review</u>
</b><br/><br/>I honestly don't know what to write on this review. This trilogy was just so perfect. So amazing and no matter how many times I reread this trilogy, I always find myself falling to it</span>
  <span id="freeText5937960791308593468" style="display:none">I am currently rereading it for the fifth times! And I’m so torn at the moment. I want to finish reading it and start reading another book in my TBR pile but I also don’t want to finish reading it at the same time because I love it too much! 😫<br><br>•••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••<br><br><b>
  <u>Fourth Time Read Review</u>
</b><br><br>I honestly don't know what to write on this review. This trilogy was just so perfect. So amazing and no matter how many times I reread this trilogy, I always find myself falling to it all over again. This trilogy indeed has a special place in my heart and I hope this will never change. <br><br>The characters development in this trilogy was also written very well. They became maturer and I could see their development. It was amazing. Sometimes it's funny to think that I haven't fallen in love with anyone in my real life but I've been loving Perry since I was 15 and a half. Maybe I sound cheesy right now lol but that's the truth. <br><br>This trilogy changed me and I'm so grateful for the changes. This trilogy inspires me to never give up and a few days ago, we had this event in my campus and I was chosen to be the speaker for a few minutes and I was so nervous and scared because that was my first time standing in front of a large crowd but I always spoke to myself that I wouldn't give up. I would do it and I just wouldn't give up. This trilogy also inspires me to spread kindness or do good things to other people. <br><br>It's been a few days since I finished reading this book but I already miss all of the characters. I will reread this trilogy again next year because this trilogy is so perfect. I recommend you all to read this trilogy and thank you so much for reading and liking this review. I hope you all have a great day! ❤️<br><br>••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••<br><b>
  <u> Third Time Read Review </u>
</b> <br><br><b>SPOILER-FREE REVIEW</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b><br>He looked back, still walking, and pressed a hand to his<br>heart.<br></b>
</blockquote><br><br>This is the third time I read this trilogy and thankfully, my feelings are exactly the same as the first and the second time I read it. I had so much fun reading this trilogy and I have binge read it for the past few weeks, so it's kind of hard for me to leave the world of this trilogy. I feel so attached to the trilogy. To the plot. To the characters. Basically everything and every time I finish this trilogy I always feel both happy and sad. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1523364171ra/25354530.gif" width="340" height="160" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>AND THIS TRILOGY STILL MANAGED TO MAKE ME CRY, EVEN THOUGH THAT IS THE THIRD TIME I READ IT. To be honest, I'm so impressed, because I used to cry a lot toward books 3 years ago, but now I don't really cry that often now. BUT THIS BOOK. DAMN. THIS BOOK TORTURED ME. I felt like the book itself punched me in the gut and said " MUAHAHAHAHA HOW DOES IT FEEL?" I don't know how many times my eyes got teary or even cried or even laughed out loud while I was reading this trilogy. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1523366148ra/25354715.gif" width="250" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>One of the things that I love from this trilogy is the friendship between a girl and a boy that <b>DOES NOT</b> end up being a couple. They care for each other and I also get this feeling that they love each other. But only as best friends and THEY ARE SO SWEET. OMG. I need a best friend like him in my real life. This is the kind of friendship that I have always looked for in books and I can't get enough of it. If you have any recommendation of platonic relationship between a boy and a girl that does not end up falling in love in the end, PLEASE DO TELL ME. <br><br>This trilogy always makes me feel a lot of emotions and no matter how many times I read it, I always feel attached to the characters. To most of them and I can relate to Aria and always agree with her. Like we have the same mind and God, I love Perry so much and I'm so relieved that my feelings toward him doesn't change, even though this is the third time I read it. I will definitely reread this trilogy again in the future, but this time I won't reread it a year later but I will reread it two years from now, because I want to forget most of the plot and the conversation in this trilogy, so I can enjoy it more. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1523370576ra/25355111.gif" width="340" height="160" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I highly recommend you to read this trilogy <b>BECAUSE IT IS SO AMAZING.</b> Thank you for reading and liking this review. I appreciate it very much and I hope you all have an amazing day! <br><br><blockquote>
  <b><br>He'd loved falling asleep with his eyes <br>on a little piece of the sky. <br></b>
</blockquote><br><br>••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••<br><br><s>
  <b>I realized that I haven't written a review for this book. So I will write one. <br><br>REVIEW TO COME. </b>
</s><br><br><br>••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••<br><b>*inhales**exhales* I'm rereading it for the third time and I AM NOT READY TO LEAVE THE WORLD OF THIS BOOK. I STILL WANT TO BE WITH MY FAVORITE CHARACTERS. AAAAAAAAAAAA</b><br>••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••<br><br>REVIEW TO COME ( maybe )</span>

<div id="review_1325162111" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1325162111" />
    <a title="Jasmine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/21803154-jasmine"><img alt="Jasmine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1582366251p2/21803154.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1325162111?book_show_action=true">Jul 04, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jasmine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jasmine" href="/user/show/21803154-jasmine">Jasmine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Everyone!</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=will-reread">will-reread</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=great-fighting-scenes">great-fighting-scenes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=highly-recommend">highly-recommend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=beautiful-stories">beautiful-stories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=ebooks-ibooks">ebooks-ibooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=happy-ending">happy-ending</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=thought-provoking">thought-provoking</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21803154-jasmine?shelf=supernatural">supernatural</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1325162111" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4144861894559599310"><b>Actual rating: 4.5/5 Unstoppable Stars</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>They had brought Dwellers and Outsiders together, and that was how it would stay.</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Before I talk about the book, I just want to say that when it comes to Perry, I can't stop thinking about <b>Chris Hemsworth</b> the whole time because of his appearance and body figure. <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454569609i/17982330._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Don't you agree he's the perfect role for him?<br/><br/>As the title indicates, <i>Into the Still Blue</i> is the last one of this series and apparently, the characters will find the Still Blue eventually. Since th</span>
  <span id="freeText4144861894559599310" style="display:none"><b>Actual rating: 4.5/5 Unstoppable Stars</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>They had brought Dwellers and Outsiders together, and that was how it would stay.</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Before I talk about the book, I just want to say that when it comes to Perry, I can't stop thinking about <b>Chris Hemsworth</b> the whole time because of his appearance and body figure. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454569609i/17982330._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Don't you agree he's the perfect role for him?<br><br>As the title indicates, <i>Into the Still Blue</i> is the last one of this series and apparently, the characters will find the Still Blue eventually. Since the result is quite obvious, what captivates me is the process in between. <blockquote>
  <b>Why was it so hard to bring together the people she loved and keep them safe? Why couldn't she just wake up and spend a day--one day--without running or fighting or losing someone?</b>
</blockquote><br>Those characters have developed into something much more memorable and seeing them grow mature is such a relief. Take Roar for example, after what he went through when such unbelievably horrible and tragic thing happened to Liv in the previous book, the only cure that can help him recover is time. Mercifully, with all the incidents in this book, he's finally able to put a big, genuine smile on his face. <blockquote>
  <b>Maybe his grief was like her wounded arm. Slowly healing. Gradually becoming less consuming as life delivered other worries and other joys. Other sources of pain and happiness.</b>
</blockquote><br>To my surprise, <b>
  <u>the author draws me into believing certain facts and thinking stereotypically of some characters at first; however, with each turning point she creates, the truth blows my mind tremendously.</u>
</b> To put it differently, I may change the way I feel about Soren, Brooke, and even Hess afterwards. But I will <b>never</b> change that about Sable. <blockquote>
  <i>Maybe he wanted to quantify Sable's ruthlessness. Futile, Perry knew. <b>He could drop a stone into the black well of Sable's heart and never hear it hit the bottom.</b></i>
</blockquote> <br>Sable's still the worst person I've seen and his wicked ideas know no boundary. A Blood Lord without heart; fake kindness along with expert manipulator are the trademarks of him. <blockquote>
  <i>He could be kind, when kindness lured a person to take a sip of poison. He could be charming and considerate. He could fool a person into believing he had a heart.</i>
</blockquote><br><i>Almost</i> everyone I've hated in the first 2 installments turned out to be just the opposite kind of people and that totally shocked me. Though some villains completely live up to my expectation of their cruelty and brutality. Thus, the entire development and transformation of the characters perfectly satisfy me here.<br>The most heartbreaking scene I experienced is all about <b>Cinder</b>. In this book, we'll learn much more information regarding the <i>Aether</i> and the <i>Still Blue.</i> Frankly, my theory about the Aether in book one was far from what it really is, but the truth impresses me a lot. Even though I know there will be <b>steep sacrifice</b> if Perry and Sable's tribes decide to break through the thick Aether and start a new leaf, the actual feeling is surreal when it was made. :(<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454569609i/17982331._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>There's no denying an impressive story involves some essential losses of good guys/warriors/brothers, and the same amount for bad ones. Therefore, when everything settles in the end, it's the spirit emitting from the survivors that nearly brings tears to my eyes. Their optimism and the way they hold a thread of hope give this series a fantasticly happy ending.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454569609i/17982332._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As for the disadvantage, in my opinion, both the inevitable sacrifice and the last bloody battle for the title of Blood Lord can be much more intensive or action-packed than they were described in the story, so the lacking of emotion is still the minor flaw in the series.<br><br>All in all, <i>Under the Never Sky</i> is a series I highly recommend to everyone and the story is indeed something worth reading. :)<br><br><u>Short Playlist</u><br>1)<a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=y2QE9j3Tciw" rel="nofollow noopener">Hilary Duff-Breathe In. Breathe Out.</a>: For what Perry had to endure throughout the book. Facing Sable. Dealing with the loss of the beloved ones. And the sacrifice.<br><br>2)<a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=jTTNWpag6fI" rel="nofollow noopener">Ellie Goulding-Army</a>: For the entire Tides, the most loyal warriors(the Six), Soren, Brooke, Marron, Molly, Roar, and Aria.<br><br>3)<a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=cxjvTXo9WWM" rel="nofollow noopener">Sia-Unstoppable</a>: Dedicated to <b>Cinder</b>, my most favorite kid in this series, and also the only one who could never be selfless enough.<br><br><u>My Expanding Thoughts</u> <b>(Optional reading for you!)</b><br>The best part of this series/book is that Veronica left us with enough space for imagination and provided me with various insights into several aspects in reality. Let me start with the basic, main concept of the story from my viewpoint. As we know, she started mentioning the Aether from the beginning of the series as if we the readers were supposed to know what it was by instinct. Not until I finished this one did I fully understand what the Aether was like. And it's the same for this extraterrestrial child, Cinder. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[He appeared tagging along Roar in the woods and then was captured because of some advantages for the Sable, and later he made the sacrifice for everyone's good, summoning the Aether to create a crack so that Perry and Sable's people could get through into the Still Blue. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> As I quoted for my topic, "they brought the Dwellers and Outsiders together and that's the way it should stay forever", I imagine the story is probably implying <b>the origin of homo-sapiens</b>, aka the beginning of human beings. Perhaps our ancestors were seperated for generations because of natural disasters(Aether here), tribes(Tides vs. Horns), social hierarchy(Dwellers vs. Outsiders)...etc. So as numerous unpeaceful centuries passed, the final survivors allied with each other to start anew. That's how the new world began.<br><br>In the meanwhile, the same notion reminded me of <b>Pangu</b> in the Chinese mythology. I'm no expert in this field, but as far as I'm concerned, Pangu seperated the sky from the earth and created the world. It's similar to the logistics of <b>Exodus</b> in the Western culture, when Moses led the Israelites from slavery in Egypt across the seperated Red Sea into the wilderness.<br><br>Lastly, this story brought out the ugliest side of humanity as well. I'm serious when I said Sable was the most cold-blooded snob; it's not his action that made me think so(well, not really) but his <i>words</i> that had me shiver and turned my blood icy cold in no time. <blockquote>
  <i>"...You know how hard it is to find trustworthy people. How impossible it is. <b>People will turn on each other for the smallest reasons. For a meal, they will toss a friendship aside. For a warm coat, they will stab each other in the back. They steal. They lie and betray. They lust for what they can't have.</b> What they do have isn't enough. We are weak, wanting creatures. We are never satisfied."</i>
</blockquote><br>I guess that's sort of true in the world we all live in, so <b>BEWARE OF THE PEOPLE AROUND YOU, GUYS! SOME OF THEM MAY BE DEVILS IN DISGUISE!!</b> *Why do I suddenly sound so evil?*<br><br>Anyway, that's all I feel when reading this series and if you're still here awake, just know that I cannot tell you how grateful I am now! Thanks for reading my longest thoughts ever and thanks for being so patient!! &lt;3*1,0000000000 times</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="4144861894559599310" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer14979151353131475794"><b>DNF</b><br/><br/>I just don't know what to say. I'm shocked. My reaction to this third and final book was so completely unexpected that I've tried several times over the past couple of months to get into it. I was sure it was just me picking it up at the wrong time and not being ready to appreciate it. But, after trying at least ten times to read this book, I've had to put it aside indefinitely. I was finding it so dull that I started skim-reading.<br/><br/>What happened?? I enjoyed <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11594257.Under_the_Never_Sky__Under_the_Never_Sky___1_' title='Under the Never Sky (Under the Never Sky, #1) by Veronica Rossi' rel='nofollow noopener'>Under the Never Sky</a> and I absolutely</span>
  <span id="freeText14979151353131475794" style="display:none"><b>DNF</b><br /><br />I just don't know what to say. I'm shocked. My reaction to this third and final book was so completely unexpected that I've tried several times over the past couple of months to get into it. I was sure it was just me picking it up at the wrong time and not being ready to appreciate it. But, after trying at least ten times to read this book, I've had to put it aside indefinitely. I was finding it so dull that I started skim-reading.<br /><br />What happened?? I enjoyed <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11594257.Under_the_Never_Sky__Under_the_Never_Sky___1_" title="Under the Never Sky (Under the Never Sky, #1) by Veronica Rossi" rel="nofollow noopener">Under the Never Sky</a> and I absolutely loved <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13253276.Through_the_Ever_Night__Under_the_Never_Sky___2_" title="Through the Ever Night (Under the Never Sky, #2) by Veronica Rossi" rel="nofollow noopener">Through the Ever Night</a>. I've been so excited for this final installment but there was nothing holding my attention. The characters I love felt flat and uninteresting... this almost never happens when I'm already invested in their stories. I found myself unable to care about Roar and Perry's grief and I couldn't care what would happen or where this book was going. <br /><br />Normally I wouldn't give more than 1 star to a book I struggled to make it halfway through, but I'm giving 2 just because I've enjoyed the first two books of this trilogy so much. So disappointing. Hopefully it's just me and other GR members won't have the same problem.</span>

There isn’t a word for you that means enough, because you’re everything to me.”<br/>“Perfect words,” she said, her smile wobbling with emotion. “Magical.</span>
  <span id="freeText7865784586958438467" style="display:none"><a href="http://thebookmaidens.blogspot.com/search/label/INTO%20THE%20STILL%20BLUE" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <i>(Update: 01/06/'14)</i>
</u><br>He leaned down, bracing his arms on either side of her, his lips soft as they kissed a trail from her mouth to her ear. “What I was trying to say,” he whispered, “is that I see you in everything. There isn’t a word for you that means enough, because you’re everything to me.”<br>“Perfect words,” she said, her smile wobbling with emotion. “Magical.”<br>He looked into her eyes, flashing a proud grin. “Yeah?...<i>
  <a href="http://thebookmaidens.blogspot.com/2014/01/teaser-4-into-still-blue-by-veronica.html" rel="nofollow noopener">read the rest on the bog</a>
</i><br><br><u>
  <i>(Update: 12/13/'13)</i>
</u><br>...<br>They came to a door flanked by Horn soldiers.<br>“Ten minutes,” Loran told them. “No one comes in that room.”<br>One of the men by the door nodded. “Yes, sir.”<br>Loran’s gaze flicked to Aria, his eyebrows knitting together. She saw dread and anticipation in his expression, and horrible thoughts crashed into her mind.<br>Until that moment, she hadn’t been afraid of him. Now she realized how naive she’d been. Loran had shown unusual interest in her the first time he’d seen her. She’d been aware of him because she’d sensed his awareness of her. She looked from the door to him, fear turning her to stone and rendering her mute.<br>... <br><br>-----------------<br><br><u>
  <i>-after reading- (Update: 12/05/'13)</i>
</u><br>Oh my.. that conclusion... it felt like rainbow after rainstorm!<br><br>------------------<br><br><u>
  <i>(Update: 12/03/'13)</i>
</u><br>Five Things That Might Surprise You About INTO THE STILL BLUE!<br>1. It was the fastest book of the trilogy to draft. (Revising is another matter.) <br>2. Roar has a tattoo along his arm/shoulder and you get to see it. (And I believe you will very much enjoy seeing it.) <br>3. Soren. <br>4. One (or more) main characters might be captured and imprisoned by the bad guys. Maybe. <br>5. I rewrote the last chapter more than any scene in the entire novel until I was finally, finally perfectly happy with it. <br><i>*(on Epic Reads's <a href="http://www.epicreads.com/blog/veronica-rossi-live-chat-recap/" rel="nofollow noopener">BLOG</a>)</i><br><br>Veronica reads a scene from Into The Steel Blue on Epic Reads live chat (a sexy scene!!) - watch the video: <a href="http://www.spreecast.com/events/tea-time-with-veronica-rossi/clips/intimate-scene-reading-with-veronica-rossi" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a><br>...<br>“I know. I know that now. It hurt both of us, but we got through it. And we’re not damaged because of it. We’re stronger.” <br>“We are?” <br>“Sure. Look at us. We’re surviving our first fight . . . or second.” <br>Aria rolled her eyes. “This isn’t a fight and neither was yesterday.” <br>He smiled. “Now you’re scaring me.” <br>She laughed. It was a sparkling sound. A burst of brightness in the quiet of the woods. For the first time since he’d seen her running toward him, he relaxed. <br>Aria still held her hand against her stomach. He wanted to take it and kiss each one of her fingers, but he didn’t want to chance making her feel worse about her injury. He stepped around her.<br>“Perry, what are you—” <br>He held her shoulders, keeping her from turning. “Trust me.”... <i>
  <a href="http://thebookmaidens.blogspot.com/2013/12/teaser-2-into-still-blue-by-veronica.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Read the rest of this scene on the Blog</a>
</i><br><i>*(the rest of the live chat: <a href="http://www.spreecast.com/events/tea-time-with-veronica-rossi" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a>)</i><br><br><u>
  <i>(Update: 07/09/'13)</i>
</u><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/permalink.php?story_fbid=471869959573091&amp;id=139136976179726" rel="nofollow noopener">Small Teaser:</a><br>Peregrine has a falcon tattoo across his back, but did you guys know that Roar has a Marking too? <br>You'll see it in INTO THE STILL BLUE. Which may or may not mean that Roar takes his shirt off. <br>Heeeee.<br>-Author, out.-<br><br>--------------<br><u>
  <i>(Update: 06/20/'13)</i>
</u><br><a href="http://www.scribd.com/fullscreen/148605732?access_key=key-19m74azue12ncsegxvtr&amp;allow_share=false&amp;show_recommendations=false" rel="nofollow noopener">THE FIRST THREE CHAPTERS!!!</a> + the cover of the US edition...<br><i>* on <a href="http://shelf-life.ew.com/2013/06/20/veronica-rossi-into-the-still-blue-cover-exclusive/" rel="nofollow noopener">EWeekly</a></i><br><br>--------------<br><u>
  <i>(Update: 04/23/'13)</i>
</u><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/permalink.php?story_fbid=438926289534125&amp;id=139136976179726" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser:</a><br>He squeezed the trigger. <br>Nothing. <br>Safety switch--something he never had to consider with a bow. He flipped it, pressed the trigger again, and didn't miss.<br><br>--------------<br><a href="http://veronicarossibooks.blogspot.com/2013/02/regarding-book-three.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Snippet:</a><br>“Yes, Molly, she is wounded and weak," Reef said, "but weakness is no longer a factor. We are all weak. What matters now is time. That is a factor. War rules. We do what's needed, when it’s needed." He pointed at Aria without looking away from Molly. "Right now that means she needs to know exactly what’s happening.”<br>Reef's words shook off any last wisp of fuzziness from Aria’s mind. They brought her back to where she’d been a week ago, alert and tense, a little breathless, with a sense of desperation curling inside of her like a stomachache.<br><i>- on Veronica Rossi's <a href="http://veronicarossibooks.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">blog</a><i></i></i></span>

<div id="review_1692013262" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1692013262" />
    <a title="Simona B" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5312173-simona-b"><img alt="Simona B" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1408893128p2/5312173.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1692013262?book_show_action=true">Jul 08, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Simona B" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Simona B" href="/user/show/5312173-simona-b">Simona B</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781907411076" href="/book/show/18071739-into-the-still-blue">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5312173-simona-b?shelf=science-fiction">science-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5312173-simona-b?shelf=in-english">in-english</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5312173-simona-b?shelf=2000">2000</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1692013262" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12764805150566647210"><b>"Try to sleep. Tomorrow’s coming, whether we worry about it or not."</b><br/><br/>•Pretty obviously, <b>the romance</b> is once again a rather <i>important</i> part of the story, and once again <b>I was more annoyed than pleased</b> by it and by the way it was handled. The only thought worth mentioning I was capable of formulating whenever Percy and Aria entered the scene was (other than "Argh please just go away") was "Go get a room and spare me your <b>ridiculous PDA</b>". And I am usually not against PDA, I even like them as long as </span>
  <span id="freeText12764805150566647210" style="display:none"><b>"Try to sleep. Tomorrow’s coming, whether we worry about it or not."</b><br /><br />•Pretty obviously, <b>the romance</b> is once again a rather <i>important</i> part of the story, and once again <b>I was more annoyed than pleased</b> by it and by the way it was handled. The only thought worth mentioning I was capable of formulating whenever Percy and Aria entered the scene was (other than "Argh please just go away") was "Go get a room and spare me your <b>ridiculous PDA</b>". And I am usually not against PDA, I even like them as long as there's a bit of moderation and enough common sense to understand where to draw a line and restrain oneself. Well, they have neither. And whether you're in her head or his, it doesn't matter, you can bet sooner or later you'll stumble upon <b>at least one paragraph per chapter</b> where <b>the other's obviously superhuman good looks are glorified</b> with praises such as "He was real and solid and beautiful" and STAHP. <br />So, yes. <b>They are insufferable</b>. On top of that, I didn not care for them the littlest bit. And I strongly feel that <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Perry's death would only have improved things <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br /><br />•I would like to add something about <b>the characters</b>, but as I have already explained, Aria and Perry seem to exist purely in relation one to the other, and all the others are little more impressive than that. No one really brought me to care.<br /><br />•I liked that <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <b>Cinder's sacrifice</b>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> in the end <b>went all the way</b> without (mock-)tragic, miraculous returns. It's not that I wouldn't have been glad for him in that case, since who we're talking about was a decent character and a nice kid, but it would only have been pathetic and of little effect. Story-wise, this way was so much better.<br /><br />•I truly am sorry, but Rossi's plots still don't convince me. The book is <b>action-packed</b> and <b>fast-paced</b>, but it all seems to me only <b>superficial</b>. For the whole trilogy, I felt like <b>things kept happening as if by inertia</b>, faintly propelled by the residue of a long-forgotten momentum. These events have no significance whatsoever, and once again, my interest was nonexistent.<br /><br />•The fact that so far I've mentioned <b>the world-building</b> only in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1612203887?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">my review of <i>Under the Never Sky</i></a> and only to express perplexity (along with no little amount of unsuccessful hopefulness) says all there is to say. It's not exactly lacking, and <b>it answers the questions it raises</b>; the thing is that those questions were not as many as I'd anticipated. From one of the most famous sci-fi ya series of the last years, <b>I expected something more elaborate</b>. <b>But it makes sense</b> and it's <b>satisfying</b> so I can easily make do with that.<br /><br />➽ Key words to understand this series (only through my eyes, of course): <b>mediocre, but enjoyable nonetheless</b>. I suggest picking it up if you are simply looking for a relazing read, don't mind if the writing style and the plot are average, and above all, if you are are keen on romance and can stand two main characters who would keep their hands on each other 24/7. <br />Good luck.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12764805150566647210" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1303654844" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1303654844" />
    <a title="Melissa (Ever So Mela)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/28640648-melissa-ever-so-mela"><img alt="Melissa (Ever So Mela)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487543962p2/28640648.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1303654844?book_show_action=true">Jun 09, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melissa (Ever So Mela)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melissa (Ever So Mela)" href="/user/show/28640648-melissa-ever-so-mela">Melissa (Ever So Mela)</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28640648-melissa-ever-so-mela?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28640648-melissa-ever-so-mela?shelf=strong-leading-lady">strong-leading-lady</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28640648-melissa-ever-so-mela?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1303654844" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14306316870020052088"><b>Full series review</b><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/987393729?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>Under the Never Sky review (book 1)</a><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1298226276?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>Through the Ever Night review (book 2)</a><br/><blockquote>I fell in love the way you fall asleep; slowly, and then all at once<br/>-John Green</blockquote><br/>The best feeling is when something takes you by surprise. When something totally unexpected happens and you're left marveling at the sight wondering how you never saw it sooner. I never expected to fall in love with this series the way I have. If those first pages were anything to go by, this series would have never seen the ins</span>
  <span id="freeText14306316870020052088" style="display:none"><b>Full series review</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/987393729?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Under the Never Sky review (book 1)</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1298226276?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Through the Ever Night review (book 2)</a><br><blockquote>I fell in love the way you fall asleep; slowly, and then all at once<br>-John Green</blockquote><br>The best feeling is when something takes you by surprise. When something totally unexpected happens and you're left marveling at the sight wondering how you never saw it sooner. I never expected to fall in love with this series the way I have. If those first pages were anything to go by, this series would have never seen the inside of my heart but as the story progressed I couldn't help but become mesmerized.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434047933i/15171111.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“We lose and lose, but we're still here. Shaking in place, afraid of doing something. I'm tired of settling for this because I don't know if something better exists. It has to. What point is there otherwise? I can do something about it now. And I will.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>I fell for Perry and his undying devotion and love. I fell for the way he cared and fought for his tribe, for his need to survive and come through on his promise that they would all make it out alive.<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Killing a man should be more different than killing a game. It was not.” </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434046620i/15171022.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I fell for Aria's resolve, her strength and loyalty. I fell for the way she grew through her challenges, for every step was a struggle but she refused to be stopped. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“She'd survived the outside. She'd survived the Aether and cannibals and wolves. She knew how to love now, and how to let go. Whatever came next, she would survive it, too” </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434046620i/15171023.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I fell for Roar's laughter and jokes, his smiles and sarcasm. I fell for his all consuming love for Liv and the friendship he strived for with Aria. I feel for his mistakes, his pain and the smiles that never reached his eyes. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Fall off your own roof."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434046620i/15171024.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I fell for Cinder's need to be loved. For Talon's faith in his uncle. For Molly's kind heart. For Brooke's redeeming soul. For Soren's mean comebacks. For Reef's grouchy behavior. For Marron's soft-hearted replies. For Liv's everlasting presence. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434045939ra/15170885.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I doubt I'll ever find a perfect series. One that has no faults or that I wouldn't change a thing. There will always be something; be it the world building or the characters, be it the ending or the unanswered questions. But when you find one that despite all errors makes your heart soar and the butterflies kick, I think that makes it worth it because all that matter in the end is if you fall. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>...And I did. Fall, I mean.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="14306316870020052088" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_513727858" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/513727858" />
    <a title="Maria" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4404986-maria"><img alt="Maria" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1299823285p2/4404986.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/513727858?book_show_action=true">Jan 22, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maria" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maria" href="/user/show/4404986-maria">Maria</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18108571-into-the-still-blue">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Maria by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/4552491-janus-the-erudite-artist">Janus the Erudite Artist</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4404986-maria?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4404986-maria?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4404986-maria?shelf=dystopia">dystopia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4404986-maria?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4404986-maria?shelf=edelweiss">edelweiss</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4404986-maria?shelf=harpercollins">harpercollins</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4404986-maria?shelf=finale">finale</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer513727858" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3703183534455035985">I recommend <a href='http://bookchilla.wordpress.com/2014/01/08/book-review-into-the-still-blue-by-veronica-rossi/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Into The Still Blue</a>.<br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13253276.Through_the_Ever_Night__Under_the_Never_Sky___2_' title='Through the Ever Night (Under the Never Sky, #2) by Veronica Rossi' rel='nofollow noopener'>Through the Ever Night</a> is much better IMO. Still, better ending than I thought possible for this series. :)<br/><br/><b>Perry</b>! <3<br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/14288998.Into_the_Still_Blue__Under_the_Never_Sky___3_' title='Into the Still Blue (Under the Never Sky, #3) by Veronica Rossi' rel='nofollow noopener'>Into the Still Blue</a> was not spectacular, to tell you the truth. Although compared to <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13125947.Reached__Matched___3_' title='Reached (Matched, #3) by Ally Condie' rel='nofollow noopener'>Reached</a>, it's more quick paced; and compared to <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/14290364.Champion__Legend___3_' title='Champion (Legend, #3) by Marie Lu' rel='nofollow noopener'>Champion</a>, it has more swoon moments.<br/><br/>The best thing about this finale is that Aria and Perry did not waste time. They took what was needed (from each other), and they did what what needs to be done (for each other). <b>Aria</b></span>
  <span id="freeText3703183534455035985" style="display:none">I recommend <a href="http://bookchilla.wordpress.com/2014/01/08/book-review-into-the-still-blue-by-veronica-rossi/" rel="nofollow noopener">Into The Still Blue</a>.<br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13253276.Through_the_Ever_Night__Under_the_Never_Sky___2_" title="Through the Ever Night (Under the Never Sky, #2) by Veronica Rossi" rel="nofollow noopener">Through the Ever Night</a> is much better IMO. Still, better ending than I thought possible for this series. :)<br /><br /><b>Perry</b>! &lt;3<br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/14288998.Into_the_Still_Blue__Under_the_Never_Sky___3_" title="Into the Still Blue (Under the Never Sky, #3) by Veronica Rossi" rel="nofollow noopener">Into the Still Blue</a> was not spectacular, to tell you the truth. Although compared to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13125947.Reached__Matched___3_" title="Reached (Matched, #3) by Ally Condie" rel="nofollow noopener">Reached</a>, it's more quick paced; and compared to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/14290364.Champion__Legend___3_" title="Champion (Legend, #3) by Marie Lu" rel="nofollow noopener">Champion</a>, it has more swoon moments.<br /><br />The best thing about this finale is that Aria and Perry did not waste time. They took what was needed (from each other), and they did what what needs to be done (for each other). <b>Aria</b> is a grown woman now, stronger and more matured than when she was still a Dweller. <b>Perry</b> is more outspoken, and more confident as the Tides blood lord, and Aria's partner.<br /><br />But. But.<br /><br /><b>Roar</b>'s character was a sore thumb. I understood his grief, but he did not understood Perry's (and how different his friend mourns for their loss). Roar went from hero to zero for me. And that's a shame!<br /><br /><b>Cinder</b> was a loose, loose end. that's it for Cinder?!!! It was a very abrupt exit for Cinder, this boy who supposedly will be their savior, the one that will usher Aether's survivors into the Still Blue. It was pretty disappointing that his character was handled carelessly, like that.<br /><br />The parts that I was so pissed about are these: <br /><br />(1) Aria's business with <b>Kirra</b> was not settled properly. I mean, c'mon on! I was eager for a cat fight!!! What a letdown. <br /><br />(2) Perry's inevitable showdown with Sable was <u>anticlimactic</u>. Lame combat, anyone? Since I first met <b>Sable</b> in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13253276.Through_the_Ever_Night__Under_the_Never_Sky___2_" title="Through the Ever Night (Under the Never Sky, #2) by Veronica Rossi" rel="nofollow noopener">Through the Ever Night</a> with Roar and Liv, I wildly anticipated his meeting with Perry. But I was in for a boring battle of the blood lords. :(<br /><br />I super loved <i>Under the Never Sky</i> series. But the finale was sort of bland, dampened down to maybe make sure that it has a neat ending. And it was, but I will not call it phenomenal.<br /><br /><i>Thank you Edelweiss and HarperCollins for granting my galley request.</i><br /><br />***<br /><br />01/22/13<br /><br />I think I can wait. Because I'm so spent after reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13253276.Through_the_Ever_Night__Under_the_Never_Sky___2_" title="Through the Ever Night (Under the Never Sky, #2) by Veronica Rossi" rel="nofollow noopener">Through the Ever Night</a>.<br /><i>Aria, let's kick Kirra's butt soon. Okay?</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="3703183534455035985" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer744201001" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14998293449570042822"><b>Into the Still Blue</b> was an amazing conclusion to a series I will hold dear to my heart! <br/><br/>We catch up with Aria and Perry after the fall of the Dwellers compound and the capture of Cinder. They have to frantically work together to save all the survivors by finding the Still Blue. But Sable is a formidable foe and a completely evil one at that. Now that he has Hess working with him and all his resources I wondered if Perry and Aria would be able to prevail. What am I saying here? Of course Veronica</span>
  <span id="freeText14998293449570042822" style="display:none"><b>Into the Still Blue</b> was an amazing conclusion to a series I will hold dear to my heart! <br /><br />We catch up with Aria and Perry after the fall of the Dwellers compound and the capture of Cinder. They have to frantically work together to save all the survivors by finding the Still Blue. But Sable is a formidable foe and a completely evil one at that. Now that he has Hess working with him and all his resources I wondered if Perry and Aria would be able to prevail. What am I saying here? Of course Veronica Rossi would not disappoint her fans! I will say that it was one hell of a ride with danger, moments of anxiousness and some heartbreak! <br /><br />One of the things I loved about this series is the lack of a love triangle. Yes Perry and Aria had their hurdles and lows to overcome but there was never a <i>serious</i> third party contender. I’m so happy Ms. Rossi stayed away from that overused and annoying plot device. (I’m looking at you Unearthly, Shatter Me, Nightshade, and The Infernal Devices!). When there were problems, they talked *gasp* and worked it out! No irritating non-communication issues! Yes, Ms. Rossi gave the YA group some credit and didn’t assume they couldn’t conduct a relationship in a healthy way! Every time Perry and Aria were together my heart raced because of the electricity of their connection. Here’s a quote that made my heart soar:<br /><b><br />“He leaned down, bracing his arms on either side of her, his lips soft as they kissed a trail from her mouth to her ear. “What I was trying to say,” he whispered, “is that I see you in everything. There isn’t a word for you that means enough, because you’re everything to me.”*</b><br /><br />Both Perry and Aria were strong and courageous on their own, and I like that their relationship didn’t diminish that. They seemed to bring out the best and root for each other; their love made each other stronger. <br /><br />When you finish a series you enjoy with characters that you adore, you can’t help but feel a twinge of sadness saying goodbye. This has been one of my favorite YA series to date, and I look forward to whatever Veronica Rossi has in store for us next! <br /><i><br />A copy was provided by Harper Collins through Edelweiss in exchange for an honest review. Thank you!</i><br /><br />*Quote taken from an uncorrected proof and may change in the final copy.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14998293449570042822" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1372782115" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1372782115" />
    <a title="Anja H." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6054186-anja-h"><img alt="Anja H." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1559051853p2/6054186.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1372782115?book_show_action=true">Aug 24, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anja H." class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anja H." href="/user/show/6054186-anja-h">Anja H.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1372782115" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2229405742940586956"><b>*4.5 ELECTRIFYING STARS*</b><br/><br/><i>"There is no way forward that isn’t through pain.”</i><br/><br/>Aaahhh, this was a great conclusion to yet another epic book trilogy that I really liked!<br/>Even though I enjoyed this series immensely, I just couldn't give this 5 stars. It just didn't touch me as deeply as some other book trilogies out there.. *cough* <s>
  <i>Daughter of Smoke and Bone</i>
</s> *cough*<br/><br/>This whole book was really fast-paced and didn't bore me for even a second! Sometimes it felt a bit rushed in my opinion, but maybe that</span>
  <span id="freeText2229405742940586956" style="display:none"><b>*4.5 ELECTRIFYING STARS*</b><br /><br /><i>"There is no way forward that isn’t through pain.”</i><br /><br />Aaahhh, this was a great conclusion to yet another epic book trilogy that I really liked!<br />Even though I enjoyed this series immensely, I just couldn't give this 5 stars. It just didn't touch me as deeply as some other book trilogies out there.. *cough* <s>
  <i>Daughter of Smoke and Bone</i>
</s> *cough*<br /><br />This whole book was really fast-paced and didn't bore me for even a second! Sometimes it felt a bit rushed in my opinion, but maybe that's because I always liked a bit more details and chit-chat in my books :)<br />Basically this book in a nutshell: reaching the Still Blue, trying to get Cinder back, getting revenge and forging alliances, all while trying to keep everyone alive and survive the worsening Aether storms. <br />Aria and Perry are definitely one of my favorite book couples of all time. Aaargh... total relationship goals right there! I could just <i>feel</i> how much they care for and love each other! My all time favorite character is Roar though. Seriously, if Roar existed in real life, I'd want him as my best friend asap! He's just so loyal, funny and true to himself, he loves really deeply and AAAARGH I can't get over him!<br />Actually, now that I think about it, I loved all the characters in these books. Yes, even Sable, just a teeny tiny bit! He's just someone who wants to be loved, accepted and respected and I can't blame him for that.<br />I'm also really glad that Aria finally got to meet her father, who is secretly also one of my new favorite characters.<br /><br />I'm so sad that some of my favorite characters died (I won't say who) but I felt that it was necessary for the story, to make it more believable and so you'll be more happy for the characters who did survive and reached the Still Blue. This book deals with a lot of hard decisions, loss, survival and revenge. It was really well executed though and I couldn't be happier with the ending!<br /><br />Overall, I really enjoyed these books and I'm totally going to read them again someday! I'd strongly recommend all YA/dystopian lovers to read this series! :)<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2229405742940586956" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_387162873" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/387162873" />
    <a title="Giselle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5789353-giselle"><img alt="Giselle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605042512p2/5789353.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/387162873?book_show_action=true">Aug 08, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Giselle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Giselle" href="/user/show/5789353-giselle">Giselle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5789353-giselle?shelf=2014">2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5789353-giselle?shelf=5-star">5-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5789353-giselle?shelf=bought-online">bought-online</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5789353-giselle?shelf=genre-apocalyptic">genre-apocalyptic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5789353-giselle?shelf=genre-action-adventure">genre-action-adventure</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5789353-giselle?shelf=age-young-adult">age-young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5789353-giselle?shelf=genre-dystopia">genre-dystopia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5789353-giselle?shelf=genre-romance">genre-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5789353-giselle?shelf=requested-for-review">requested-for-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5789353-giselle?shelf=genre-science-fiction">genre-science-fiction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer387162873" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14393353884623923270">There’s just something about Veronica Rossi’s writing that makes you forget about your own life. You find yourself transported into its pages and I love that feeling. In this case, I was psyched to read this. The final book in the trilogy starts off with a revelation that there could be a place without the storm. A place where they could all be safe and free from the storms that surge in the sky.<br/><br/>Aria and Perry search for this place throughout the book, and they end up finding answers to some que</span>
  <span id="freeText14393353884623923270" style="display:none">There’s just something about Veronica Rossi’s writing that makes you forget about your own life. You find yourself transported into its pages and I love that feeling. In this case, I was psyched to read this. The final book in the trilogy starts off with a revelation that there could be a place without the storm. A place where they could all be safe and free from the storms that surge in the sky.<br /><br />Aria and Perry search for this place throughout the book, and they end up finding answers to some questions they've been meaning to answer. In Roar’s case, it’s about his loved one, who just so happens to be Perry’s sister. I felt so much sympathy for Roar in this one. Hurting like he did and still trying to live day by day couldn’t have been easy. He’s so different in this one, so broken and it didn’t even feel the same. He wasn’t cracking as many jokes or laughing. A side to his character that shows how much he’s grown or in this case, how much he’s experienced.<br /><br />This one was one page turner, and I just loved the ending. At one point, it felt like it did end, but you realize there’s more pages so that was a rare treat. Usually books just end in an instant without any more to go on. Not in this case, because we get to see what is to come for their future.<br /><br />I’m sad this trilogy has ended, but I’m also wanting more from it. I believe there’s a novella with Roar so that’s just one other thing I can’t wait to grab my hands on.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14393353884623923270" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer16496754710427532824">Two words that describe this book: beautiful and tragic. <br/><br/> i can't believe it's the end of this series. This series has been sitting on my shelves for like a year or a two and tell you what, i've only gotten myself to go give it a chance like last week and it was worth it.   <span id="freeText16496754710427532824" style="display:none">Two words that describe this book: beautiful and tragic. <br /><br /> i can't believe it's the end of this series. This series has been sitting on my shelves for like a year or a two and tell you what, i've only gotten myself to go give it a chance like last week and it was worth it. Totally. <br /><br />The plot was utterly well studied and how I was amazed by Rossi's writing style. The pacing of the novel was quite good, I mean really good. I swear. <br /><br />There are no boring moments. Everyone single character of this series has touched my soul. That everything about them makes them family except from blood.<br /><br />How I even grew fond of the protagonists for they played their roles well. That I sometimes want to hug them and punch them and throw them into the wolves and hope that they won't come back leading them. <br /><br />From the dedication up to the acknowledgement, it was worth reading it. This world was cruel yet magical. It makes me wonder of what future might become. <br /><br />The twist and turns of the story totally hooked me. So many revelations. If only my sister was not sitting next to me, I would've cried many times because this book was just so beautiful yet heartbreaking. <br /><br />And news flash: there were so many death. I did not expect them and a lot of them made my eyes water for a little. And believe me, I found myself asking the author why the hell did she murdered these sweet innocent fictional characters? How? Howwwwww?!???! <br /><br />Though I have to say, I love the budding romance between Soren and Brooke like emeghed. They're so cute!! <br /><br />Even though the ending was rushed! I still enjoyed it!! The scenes in where Perry and Aria swam in order to get to this certain cave was golden! And the scene where Perry was taking of his pants then Aria entered the room was utterly hilarious. That made me closed the book for a while and laugh maniacally. My god! I need to go to the church. <br /><br />The farewell scenes in where all of them thought that they were not going to see each other broke my heart. My heart was crushed at that moment and PAK U SABLE! <br /><br />PLEASE STOP READING THIS IF YOU STILL HAVEN't read this book! Please! I beg of u! I don't want u to be like me who is always curious and do not follow this. PLEASE STOP READING BECAUSE SPOILERS AHEAD. <br /><br />I AM SO FUCKING PISSED THAT CINDER DIED. I WAS KINDA HOPING FOR A TWIST THAT HE DID MANAGED TO SURVIVE BUT NO! He did not and that still made me want to cry! Up to now, while my stupid hands dance across this stupid keypad. <br /><br />I WAS SHIPPING HIM WITH WILLOW! And come to think of it! What will happen with Willow? Will she meet a boy in the Horns tribe? Like dudeee!!! :((( <br /><br />I AM STILL FUCKING SAD AND ANGRY THAT CINDER DIED AND REEF. <br /><br />Reef was everything!! He acted as a father and a loyal advisor to Perry when he needed one the most. Sure, he acted like a jerk at like the beginning of book two but I don't care! <br /><br />I AM MOURNING FOR THE DEATH OF THEM!!!!!!!!<br /><br /><br />And I also kinda felt sad that Hess died! Sure, he was evil and such but at least he turned away from the dark side like Darth Vader and that's what matters! HE DIED FIGHTING! Fighting for his people!!!</span>

  <b>The trilogy-ending curse has been broken.</b>

I had been expecting one thing, and when I got something else, I think I balked at it without realizing. Once I got over the fact that the character-driven vibe of the past two books wasn't going to be as strong of a factor here, I settled in to enjoy the one thing that I always </span>
  <span id="freeText5455259747033564953" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390931536i/8299935.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>The trilogy-ending curse has been broken.</b>
</blockquote><br>Now I get why it took me 3 tries to finally buckle down and read <i>Into the Still Blue</i>. The final installment was good in its own right, but it was very different in execution. I had been expecting one thing, and when I got something else, I think I balked at it without realizing. Once I got over the fact that the character-driven vibe of the past two books wasn't going to be as strong of a factor here, I settled in to enjoy the one thing that I always say YA sci-fi books need more of : <i>actual</i> sci-fi. <br><br>While I still missed some of what made UTNS and TTEN so special to me, I understood why the trilogy ending needed to branch off and kick some ass.<br><br>All in all, this was a satisfying (okay, so one thing could have been more satisfying...but I get it...sigh) end to an excellent trilogy. Well done, Ms. Rossi. <br><br><i>This book provided from the publisher in exchange for an honest review.</i><br></span>

<div id="review_1780821888" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1780821888" />
    <a title="Jen ♥Star-Crossed Book Blog♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog"><img alt="Jen ♥Star-Crossed Book Blog♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576986930p2/28353412.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1780821888?book_show_action=true">Oct 10, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen ♥Star-Crossed Book Blog♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen ♥Star-Crossed Book Blog♥" href="/user/show/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog">Jen ♥Star-Crossed Book Blog♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18108571-into-the-still-blue">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=insta-not-used">insta-not-used</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=good-boys-i-love">good-boys-i-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=sigh-bbf">sigh-bbf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=science-fiction">science-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=dont-cry">dont-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1780821888" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14946967713024295318"><b>*Spoilers for previous books*</b><br/><br/><b>Into the Still Blue was an action packed, stunning conclusion! </b>And just like the two previous books, this story was an emotional journey. Torture, love, sacrifice, it honestly felt like my heart would stop beating at times. Even while they were strategizing, since the risks they were willing to take felt monumental. <b>This series has easily become one of my favorite dystopian series ever, and I can't recommend it highly enough!</b><br/><blockquote>
  
    <b>Why was it so hard to bring togeth</b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText14946967713024295318" style="display:none"><b>*Spoilers for previous books*</b><br><br><b>Into the Still Blue was an action packed, stunning conclusion! </b>And just like the two previous books, this story was an emotional journey. Torture, love, sacrifice, it honestly felt like my heart would stop beating at times. Even while they were strategizing, since the risks they were willing to take felt monumental. <b>This series has easily become one of my favorite dystopian series ever, and I can't recommend it highly enough!</b><br><blockquote>
  
    <b>Why was it so hard to bring together the people she loved and keep them safe? Why couldn’t she just wake up and spend a day—</b>
    <b>
      <i>one</i>
    </b>
    <b> day—without running or fighting or losing someone?</b>
  
</blockquote><br><b>I started out this book feeling overwhelmed. Their situation had become dire.</b> The Tides and Dwellers were about to become trapped in the cave and die because of how the aether was changing. They <i>had</i> to find the Still Blue! But to do that they needed hoovers and Cinder, which were both in the custody of Hess and Sable. <b>And while that seemed daunting enough, their relationships with one another were all twisted. Roar, Aria, Perry. Nothing felt right. </b> Oh. My. Gosh. I just wanted to curl into a ball and cry with how much each of them were struggling or suffering or pretending that they weren't. I felt suffocated from their drama, but thankfully there was an awesome distraction coming up!<br><blockquote>
  
    <b>“Soren,” Roar called. When Soren looked back, Roar flung his knife into the air. The blade spun end over end, heading right for Soren, who yelped and dodged aside.<br> It missed him by a hair, as Roar had surely intended. Roar never missed.<br> “Are you insane?” Soren yelled, his face turning red.<br> Roar jogged over and calmly picked up his knife, but he sheathed the blade with a vicious thrust. “That’s how you do a warning shot.”</b>
  
</blockquote><br><b>They had to form a team to rescue Cinder and obtain more hoovers. Hmm, I guess I should rephrase that, an unlikely team. </b> Perry, Aria, Roar, Soren, Brooke and Jupiter. I definitely was uncertain about this, because <b>while each of them was perfect for the mission, together they were not a good mesh. They fought. They didn't always work together. And they screwed up because of those issues.</b> But I will say that I found hope. Aria played a joke on Soren, which made me laugh so hard. And that moment led to that hope. Hope that this mismatched team would pull together and make not only everyone else, but themselves proud too! I mean, everyone's survival rests on their shoulders. No biggie right?<br><blockquote>
  
    <b>“If we get to the Still Blue,” Soren said, “we should look at how to make more people like you, Aria.”<br> She laughed. “</b>
    <b>
      <i>Make</i>
    </b>
    <b> more people like me? You mean half-breeds?”<br> “No. I mean people who are forgiving and optimistic and things like that.”</b>
  
</blockquote><br><b><br> I have to say a word about each character that affected me so strongly:</b><br><br><b>Aria &amp; Perry</b> - She made me so proud with the strategizing she came up with. Her and Perry have grown immensely since their first encounter. And Perry now felt like a true leader. The decisions and sacrifices he made, I'm so proud of him, even if I still can't talk about it.<br><br><b>Roar</b> - I never thought I'd find two book boyfriends in a story. But I absolutely loved Roar. Even when he was being an emotional ass. I will never be able to get him out of my head.<br><br><b>Soren </b>- That dweller pulled me in, no matter how hard I fought it. He completely won me over and I was hoping he got a HEA too!<br><br><b>Cinder</b> - He started out as a tag along, and in the Tides he finally found what he was always searching for. A family. He was braver than I ever could have been at his age, and I loved his moments throughout the story.<br><blockquote>
  
    <b>Aria didn’t even see Perry’s face before he hugged her. “I’ll be thinking about you,” he said, lifting her off the ground. “I love you.”<br> She said it back, and that was it.<br> All that mattered. Everything there was to say.</b>
  
</blockquote><br>The twists and turns kept me on my toes, but the events that unfolded and affected the characters, that's what moved my heart so deeply. I sobbed. I pleaded. I hoped they would all survive. Even though I <i>should</i> have known better. <b>This story was perfectly destructive and uplifting at the same time. And I won't be able to get their world or these characters out of my head for a long time to come.</b><br><br>PS Can we please have a novella looking into the future? My heart desperately needs that!<br><br><i>For more of my reviews, please visit:</i> <br><a title="Star-Crossed Book Blog" href="http://starcrossedbookblog.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="200" width="320" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452287496i/17673736._SX540_.jpg" alt="descriptive text here" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <u>
  <b> </b>
</u><br><a title="Facebook" href="https://www.facebook.com/starcrossedbookblog" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1438055977i/15660595.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/994815796" />
    <a title="Lotte" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25309949-lotte"><img alt="Lotte" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1408555448p2/25309949.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/994815796?book_show_action=true">Jul 13, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lotte" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lotte" href="/user/show/25309949-lotte">Lotte</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25309949-lotte?shelf=ge-dystopian-fiction">ge-dystopian-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25309949-lotte?shelf=a-young-adult-fiction">a-young-adult-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25309949-lotte?shelf=2015-priority">2015-priority</a>,
