        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer994815796" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9709424677899470742">Are you looking for an entertaining dystopian trilogy that doesn't get progressively worse with each book? Then look no further! The Under the Never Sky trilogy might be exactly what you're looking for! Some things that speak for these books: solid world building that doesn't completely fall apart in the last book; a cute and in its own way even kind of realistic romance (and I'm usually not one to swoon over romances in YA dystopias); an awesome platonic (!) friendship between a guy and a girl </span>
  <span id="freeText9709424677899470742" style="display:none">Are you looking for an entertaining dystopian trilogy that doesn't get progressively worse with each book? Then look no further! The Under the Never Sky trilogy might be exactly what you're looking for! Some things that speak for these books: solid world building that doesn't completely fall apart in the last book; a cute and in its own way even kind of realistic romance (and I'm usually not one to swoon over romances in YA dystopias); an awesome platonic (!) friendship between a guy and a girl (pretty unique for this genre!) and a great plot that takes some twists and turns along the way. The story itself isn't the most original and follows the general recipe for YA dystopias, plus, the story becomes pretty angsty at times, but all in all, I think that this trilogy is worth your time and I'd definitely recommend it!</span>
  <a data-text-id="9709424677899470742" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

They remained true to themselves though, and it is so amazing. I just can't rave about this series enough!<br/>I love this world, it's so creative and interesting. <div id="review_720014532" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/720014532" />
    <a title="Melanie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10890208-melanie"><img alt="Melanie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1413275441p2/10890208.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/720014532?book_show_action=true">Sep 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melanie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melanie" href="/user/show/10890208-melanie">Melanie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10890208-melanie?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10890208-melanie?shelf=e-arc">e-arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10890208-melanie?shelf=not-bad-at-all">not-bad-at-all</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10890208-melanie?shelf=action">action</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10890208-melanie?shelf=dystopian-utopian">dystopian-utopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10890208-melanie?shelf=death">death</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10890208-melanie?shelf=swoony-guys">swoony-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10890208-melanie?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10890208-melanie?shelf=kick-ass-character">kick-ass-character</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10890208-melanie?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer720014532" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17654164104438719539">See more reviews at <a href='http://yamidnightreads.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>YA Midnight Reads</a><br/><br/>Into The Still Blue is the final conclusion to the Under the Never Sky trilogy and delivered a lot of kick-assery, sweet romance, unforgettable friendships and higher stakes for all the characters. And as a last instalment does, Veronica Rossi adds to this mix with some heartbreak, second chances and sacrifices.<br/><br/>Our two main characters, Perry and Aria were both fantastic narrators and have both come so far. Perry’s bravery and leadership is strong and I enjoye</span>
  <span id="freeText17654164104438719539" style="display:none">See more reviews at <a href="http://yamidnightreads.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">YA Midnight Reads</a><br /><br />Into The Still Blue is the final conclusion to the Under the Never Sky trilogy and delivered a lot of kick-assery, sweet romance, unforgettable friendships and higher stakes for all the characters. And as a last instalment does, Veronica Rossi adds to this mix with some heartbreak, second chances and sacrifices.<br /><br />Our two main characters, Perry and Aria were both fantastic narrators and have both come so far. Perry’s bravery and leadership is strong and I enjoyed his determination to get to the Still Blue. As for Aria, she has the longest way. She used to be an innocent and weak girl who didn’t know how to handle a knife, but now she’s a badass chick ready to fight with all the strength she has in her. The romance is equally brilliant; there were barely any miscommunications, and when there were, Perry and Aria they talked it out. This is what a genuine relationship is like! Veronica Rossi creates such authentic and three dimensional characters, they really cling onto you and never let go even once the story has ended.<br /><br />Along with Perry and Aria, there’s also the beloved Roar. We see a different side to him in Into The Still Blue, he is grieving and utterly lost after what happened to Liv, most of the time just sitting there, staring at nothing. While he could’ve turned into a whiny character, he didn’t. Veronica Rossi portrays his sadness and loss realistically; I even started to feel my own blanket of sadness covering me. What Veronica Rossi does best is creating the ultimate, platonic friendship between a girl and a boy. Aria and Roar’s friendship was complete romance free and I absolutely loved it their interactions. They help each other through tough situations and give advice to each other (including love advice); it’s absolutely amazing and still hilarious despite Roar’s slightly more sorrowful demeanour. I am still waiting for another author to make a friendship like Veronica Rossi’s.<br /><br />After the epic second instalment Veronica Rossi delivered, I’ll be honest and say that I did expect her conclusion to the Under the Never Sky series to be grander and end with more of a ‘bang’. I felt that the ending of this book was rushed and many things that I had wildly anticipating for most of the book wasn’t made so <i>significant </i>when the time came. Yes, I wanted more of a dramatic feel; I wanted my heart to rush till the very end. I wanted a better climax.<br /><br />Even though the ending was weaker than I had wanted it to be, Into The Still Blue was still a wonderful last instalment, saying a last goodbye to our favourite characters. I definitely will be on the lookout for more of this author’s works; they are just bound to be wonderful.<br /><p>
  <em>~Thank you HarperTeen for sending me this copy!~</em>
</p> </span>
  <a data-text-id="17654164104438719539" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Jon" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4277731-jon"><img alt="Jon" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1384212540p2/4277731.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/445765364?book_show_action=true">Oct 31, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jon" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jon" href="/user/show/4277731-jon">Jon</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4277731-jon?shelf=dystopia-post-apocalyptic">dystopia-post-apocalyptic</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<div id="review_798032138" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/798032138" />
    <a title="Ferdy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4596358-ferdy"><img alt="Ferdy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487898103p2/4596358.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/798032138?book_show_action=true">Dec 23, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ferdy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ferdy" href="/user/show/4596358-ferdy">Ferdy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=powers">powers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=rubbish-ending">rubbish-ending</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=predictable">predictable</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=boring-crap-hero">boring-crap-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=liar-hero">liar-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=blah-romance">blah-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=awful-love-interest">awful-love-interest</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=cheating-hero">cheating-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer798032138" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5540957227499638199"><b>2.5 stars - Spoilers</b><br/><br/>This was more enjoyable than <i>Through the Ever Night</i> (though that's not saying much since I didn't like that), it was far more action packed, cohesive, and gripping. But there were certain aspects that I had issues with such as the predictability, and the slow middle section, also Perry's character and the romance grated on me (a lot).<br/><br/>-<i>Into the Still Blue</i> was essentially about Aria and Perry trying to save both their people (the Dwellers and Outsiders) from the increasingly de</span>
  <span id="freeText5540957227499638199" style="display:none"><b>2.5 stars - Spoilers</b><br /><br />This was more enjoyable than <i>Through the Ever Night</i> (though that's not saying much since I didn't like that), it was far more action packed, cohesive, and gripping. But there were certain aspects that I had issues with such as the predictability, and the slow middle section, also Perry's character and the romance grated on me (a lot).<br /><br />-<i>Into the Still Blue</i> was essentially about Aria and Perry trying to save both their people (the Dwellers and Outsiders) from the increasingly deadly Aether storms. They could only do that by finding the Still Blue, a place free from Aether. <br /><br />-Before Aria and the gang could do anything though they had to find the ships that would take their people to safety. Unfortunately, the ships were with Hess and Sable… So they had to outsmart them and steal them. It was all pretty interesting with Aria and co fighting and trying to outmaneuver Sable and Hess… But once the gang were face to face with Sable and Hess, the story got really repetitive and slow, and most of the characters just acted angsty and felt sorry for themselves. It was only the last third or so where things kicked in and picked up again.<br /><br />-I'm not usually a fan of dual POV, the two narrators always end up sounding exactly the same. The dual perspective was done quite well in this, it was easy for me to differentiate between Aria and Perry's voices. Unfortunately, since I loathed Perry, I disliked all his chapters. To be honest, I would have much preferred reading just from Aria's POV.<br /><br />-I enjoyed the parts where the Dwellers and Outsiders worked together to survive, they were both useful in their own ways. Without Soren/Aria/the Dwellers the Outsiders wouldn't have been able use the technology and ships that were needed to take everyone to the Still Blue. And without Perry/Roar/the Outsiders the Dwellers wouldn't have managed to fight and survive in the world outside the pods. It was good having all the characters mix with each other properly, I liked Brooke and Soren's little flirtation, even though they were from different worlds they weirdly suited each other.<br /><br />-Aria was a decent character, she didn't whine or moan nearly as much as most other YA heroines. She was loyal, she wasn't TSTL, she took action when needed, and she was determined to help everyone. The best thing about her was her friendship with Roar, they were so natural and sweet with each other, I was desperately hoping they'd end up together because there were so much better than Perry and Aria's rubbish relationship.<br /><br />-I hated Perry, he was an awful character… He was a lying, cheating, self-pitying loser. He never once admitted all his wrongdoings, he always had an excuse, and thought that everyone else was at fault. He didn't even grieve for his dead sister or support his supposed best friend when he was going through hell, nobody else's feeling were as important as his. He didn't deserve Aria or Roar, he cared more about himself than he did them.<br /><br />-Perry was such a douche to Aria, after she risked her life so she could find his missing nephew all Perry did was bitch and whine at her — he wasn't grateful for what she did, and he had no faith in her whatsoever. Instead of thanking Aria for reuniting him with his beloved nephew, he just made her feel guilty for leaving him. He never once said how happy he was that she managed to find his only remaining family, he just gave her a hard time and made her feel like rubbish. At least Aria never cheated on him or betrayed him, whereas Perry was all hot and bothered about another girl (Kirra) five minutes after Aria left him so she could save his nephew. It was disgusting that Perry lorded all of Aria's wrongdoings over her but not once did he mention his attraction, his emotional cheating, or all the heated moments he had with Kirra. He kept it secret even when Kirra turned up again to cause havoc - Aria had a right to know about how much Perry wanted Kirra, how she made him feel lusty, and how he was all over her… But he said nothing. He was vile. I have no doubt that he'll cheat on Aria again when they're going through a rough patch and some hot girl is flirting with him — he has no loyalty to Aria and he loves being all over other girls more than he loves Aria.<br /><br />-Was it meant to be sweet when Perry told Aria he'd give her one of his arrows as a gift? He'd already given one to Brooke when he was dating her so yea, it wasn't sweet or swoon-worthy when he'd already done the exact same thing with his ex.<br /><br />-I was disappointed with the fact that all Aria's important relationships were with male characters… she only seemed to care about Perry, Roar, Talon, her dad, and Marron. She didn't really have one close female friend her own age, the only female character that she did properly get along was Molly who was in her sixties, and even then they hardly interacted.<br /><br />-Aria's dad was a douche, his whole attitude pissed me off. He was more worried about following Sable's orders and his own welfare than his daughter. The fact that he knew he had a teenage daughter but had never tried to contact her or check to see if she was safe and happy just showed how little he cared for Aria. I rolled my eyes when he acted all hurt about Aria's mum dying, he left her when she was pregnant and didn't give her another thought in almost two decades… As if he cared about her. I was hoping he'd die a horrible death but instead he got to a new life and a devoted daughter who he didn't even raise.<br /><br />-I wasn't happy at all with Cinder's end, he felt like a deus ex machinas. He didn't have a journey of his own, he was just there to save everyone else with his super speshul powers. As soon as he saved the day he was killed off and forgotten about. I wanted more from his character.<br /><br />All in all, I had mixed feelings for this - I liked most of the characters but I hated Perry and his POV, Roar and Aria's friendship was lovely but Perry and Aria's romance was awful, and the pace was fast apart from in the middle where nothing happened. I'm still undecided as to whether I'll be reading any future releases from the author.<br /><br />**ARC from Edelweiss<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5540957227499638199" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

		<td>
		    <b>
          <a title="Colleen Houck Book Club" class="actionLink" href="https://www.goodreads.com/topic/show/1838806-live-chat-with-veronica-rossi">Colleen Houck Boo...:</a>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('xcsH+XwxbGUJ8Cjxk1D/zIRhzoaU6DlNhBU3TL/dQajuBPzunI3337uElr9bEaQ9XOSaX/k1g2W2U3zGNPqmqg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('GIypWAR565YYvj3nVRrvvW44YeB2Gw7a520rIX7+XNozQ1JP5MVwLKrKg6mdW7RMtr01ORvGtPLVK2Cr9dm72A==')})
  }
